THE MARRIAGE ACT
(No. 4 of 2014)
MINISTERS LICENSED TO CELEBRATE MARRIAGES
NOTICE is given that in exercise of the powers conferred by section 52 of the Marriage Act, 2014, the Ministers of faith named in the Schedule hereto have been licensed to celebrate marriages under the provisions of the said Act.
